root/sysdeps/x86_64/fpu/multiarch/svml_d_tan8_core_avx512.S

  12    MERCHANTABILITY or FITNESS FOR A PARTICULAR PURPOSE.  See the GNU

  16    License along with the GNU C Library; if not, see
  17    https://www.gnu.org/licenses/.  */
  18 
  19 /*
  20  * ALGORITHM DESCRIPTION:
  21  *
  22  *      ( optimized for throughput, with small table lookup, works when HW FMA is available )
  23  *
  24  *      Implementation reduces argument x to |R|<pi/32
  25  *      16-entry tables used to store high and low parts of tan(x0)
  26  *      Argument x = N*pi + x0 + (R);   x0 = k*pi/16, with k in {0, 1, ..., 15}
  27  *      (very large arguments reduction resolved in _vdreduction_core.i)
  28  *      Compute result as (tan(x0) + tan(R))/(1-tan(x0)*tan(R))
  29  *      High accuracy ( < 1 ulp ) version keeps extra precision for numerator, denominator, and during
  30  *      final NR-iteration computing quotient.
  31  *
  32  *
  33  */
  34 
  35 /* Offsets for data table __svml_dtan_data_internal
  36  */
  37 #define _dInvPI_uisa                    0
  38 #define _dPI1_uisa                      64
  39 #define _dPI2_uisa                      128
  40 #define _dPI3_uisa                      192
  41 #define Th_tbl_uisa                     256
  42 #define _dPC3_uisa                      384
  43 #define _dPC5_uisa                      448
  44 #define _dPC7_uisa                      512
  45 #define _dPC9_uisa                      576
  46 #define _dPC11_uisa                     640
  47 #define _dOne_uisa                      704
  48 #define _dAbsMask                       768
  49 #define _dRangeVal                      832
  50 #define _dRShift                        896
  51 #define _dReductionRangeVal             960
  52 #define _dPI1                           1024
  53 #define _dPI2                           1088
  54 #define _dPI3                           1152
  55 
  56 #include <sysdep.h>
  57 
  58         .text
  59     .section .text.evex512,"ax",@progbits
  60 ENTRY(_ZGVeN8v_tan_skx)
  61         pushq     %rbp
  62         cfi_def_cfa_offset(16)
  63         movq      %rsp, %rbp
  64         cfi_def_cfa(6, 16)
  65         cfi_offset(6, -16)
  66         andq      $-64, %rsp
  67         subq      $192, %rsp
  68         xorl      %edx, %edx
  69 
  70 /* Large values check */
  71         vmovups   _dReductionRangeVal+__svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %zmm1
  72 
  73 /*
  74  *
  75  * Main path
  76  *
  77  * start arg. reduction
  78  */
  79         vmovups   _dRShift+__svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %zmm2
  80         vmovups   _dPI1_uisa+__svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %zmm5
  81         vmovups   _dPI2_uisa+__svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %zmm3
  82         vmovups   _dPI3_uisa+__svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %zmm4
  83         vmovaps   %zmm0, %zmm11
  84         vandpd    _dAbsMask+__svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %zmm11, %zmm0
  85         vcmppd    $22, {sae}, %zmm1, %zmm0, %k1
  86         vmovups   __svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %zmm1
  87 
  88 /*
  89  *
  90  * End of main path
  91  */
  92 
  93         kortestw  %k1, %k1
  94         vfmadd213pd {rn-sae}, %zmm2, %zmm11, %zmm1
  95         vsubpd    {rn-sae}, %zmm2, %zmm1, %zmm8
  96         vfnmadd213pd {rn-sae}, %zmm11, %zmm8, %zmm5
  97         vfnmadd231pd {rn-sae}, %zmm8, %zmm3, %zmm5
  98         vfnmadd213pd {rn-sae}, %zmm5, %zmm4, %zmm8
  99 
 100 /* Go to auxilary branch */
 101         jne       L(AUX_BRANCH)
 102                                 # LOE rbx r12 r13 r14 r15 edx zmm0 zmm1 zmm8 zmm11 k1
 103 
 104 /* Return from auxilary branch
 105  * for out of main path inputs
 106  */
 107 
 108 L(AUX_BRANCH_RETURN):
 109         vmovups   Th_tbl_uisa+__svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %zmm0
 110         vmovups   _dPC9_uisa+__svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %zmm5
 111         vmovups   _dPC7_uisa+__svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %zmm2
 112         vmovups   _dPC5_uisa+__svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %zmm3
 113         vmovups   _dPC3_uisa+__svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %zmm4
 114         vmulpd    {rn-sae}, %zmm8, %zmm8, %zmm6
 115         vpermt2pd Th_tbl_uisa+64+__svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %zmm1, %zmm0
 116         vmovups   _dPC11_uisa+__svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %zmm1
 117         vfmadd231pd {rn-sae}, %zmm6, %zmm1, %zmm5
 118         vfmadd213pd {rn-sae}, %zmm2, %zmm6, %zmm5
 119         vfmadd213pd {rn-sae}, %zmm3, %zmm6, %zmm5
 120         vfmadd213pd {rn-sae}, %zmm4, %zmm6, %zmm5
 121         vmulpd    {rn-sae}, %zmm8, %zmm5, %zmm7
 122         vfmadd213pd {rn-sae}, %zmm8, %zmm6, %zmm7
 123 
 124 /*
 125  * Computer Denominator:
 126  * dDenominator - dDlow ~= 1-(dTh+dTl)*(dP+dPlow)
 127  */
 128         vmovups   _dOne_uisa+__svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %zmm8
 129 
 130 /*
 131  * Compute Numerator:
 132  * dNumerator + dNlow ~= dTh+dTl+dP+dPlow
 133  */
 134         vaddpd    {rn-sae}, %zmm0, %zmm7, %zmm9
 135         vfnmadd213pd {rn-sae}, %zmm8, %zmm7, %zmm0
 136 
 137 /*
 138  * Now computes (dNumerator + dNlow)/(dDenominator - dDlow)
 139  * Choose NR iteration instead of hardware division
 140  */
 141         vrcp14pd  %zmm0, %zmm10
 142 
 143 /* One NR iteration to refine dRcp */
 144         vfnmadd231pd {rn-sae}, %zmm10, %zmm0, %zmm8
 145         vfmadd213pd {rn-sae}, %zmm10, %zmm8, %zmm10
 146         vmulpd    {rn-sae}, %zmm9, %zmm10, %zmm12
 147 
 148 /* One NR iteration to refine dQuotient */
 149         vfmsub213pd {rn-sae}, %zmm9, %zmm12, %zmm0
 150         vfnmadd213pd {rn-sae}, %zmm12, %zmm10, %zmm0
 151         testl     %edx, %edx
 152 
 153 /* Go to special inputs processing branch */
 154         jne       L(SPECIAL_VALUES_BRANCH)
 155                                 # LOE rbx r12 r13 r14 r15 edx zmm0 zmm11
 156 
 157 /* Restore registers
 158  * and exit the function
 159  */
 160 
 161 L(EXIT):
 162         movq      %rbp, %rsp
 163         popq      %rbp
 164         cfi_def_cfa(7, 8)
 165         cfi_restore(6)
 166         ret
 167         cfi_def_cfa(6, 16)
 168         cfi_offset(6, -16)
 169 
 170 /* Branch to process
 171  * special inputs
 172  */
 173 
 174 L(SPECIAL_VALUES_BRANCH):
 175         vmovups   %zmm11, 64(%rsp)
 176         vmovups   %zmm0, 128(%rsp)
 177                                 # LOE rbx r12 r13 r14 r15 edx zmm0
 178 
 179         xorl      %eax, %eax
 180                                 # LOE rbx r12 r13 r14 r15 eax edx
 181 
 182         vzeroupper
 183         movq      %r12, 16(%rsp)
 184         /*  DW_CFA_expression: r12 (r12) (DW_OP_lit8; DW_OP_minus; DW_OP_const4s: -64; DW_OP_and; DW_OP_const4s: -176; DW_OP_plus)  */
 185         .cfi_escape 0x10, 0x0c, 0x0e, 0x38, 0x1c, 0x0d, 0xc0, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0x1a, 0x0d, 0x50, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0x22
 186         movl      %eax, %r12d
 187         movq      %r13, 8(%rsp)
 188         /*  DW_CFA_expression: r13 (r13) (DW_OP_lit8; DW_OP_minus; DW_OP_const4s: -64; DW_OP_and; DW_OP_const4s: -184; DW_OP_plus)  */
 189         .cfi_escape 0x10, 0x0d, 0x0e, 0x38, 0x1c, 0x0d, 0xc0, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0x1a, 0x0d, 0x48, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0x22
 190         movl      %edx, %r13d
 191         movq      %r14, (%rsp)
 192         /*  DW_CFA_expression: r14 (r14) (DW_OP_lit8; DW_OP_minus; DW_OP_const4s: -64; DW_OP_and; DW_OP_const4s: -192; DW_OP_plus)  */
 193         .cfi_escape 0x10, 0x0e, 0x0e, 0x38, 0x1c, 0x0d, 0xc0, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0x1a, 0x0d, 0x40, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0x22
 194                                 # LOE rbx r15 r12d r13d
 195 
 196 /* Range mask
 197  * bits check
 198  */
 199 
 200 L(RANGEMASK_CHECK):
 201         btl       %r12d, %r13d
 202 
 203 /* Call scalar math function */
 204         jc        L(SCALAR_MATH_CALL)
 205                                 # LOE rbx r15 r12d r13d
 206 
 207 /* Special inputs
 208  * processing loop
 209  */
 210 
 211 L(SPECIAL_VALUES_LOOP):
 212         incl      %r12d
 213         cmpl      $8, %r12d
 214 
 215 /* Check bits in range mask */
 216         jl        L(RANGEMASK_CHECK)
 217                                 # LOE rbx r15 r12d r13d
 218 
 219         movq      16(%rsp), %r12
 220         cfi_restore(12)
 221         movq      8(%rsp), %r13
 222         cfi_restore(13)
 223         movq      (%rsp), %r14
 224         cfi_restore(14)
 225         vmovups   128(%rsp), %zmm0
 226 
 227 /* Go to exit */
 228         jmp       L(EXIT)
 229         /*  DW_CFA_expression: r12 (r12) (DW_OP_lit8; DW_OP_minus; DW_OP_const4s: -64; DW_OP_and; DW_OP_const4s: -176; DW_OP_plus)  */
 230         .cfi_escape 0x10, 0x0c, 0x0e, 0x38, 0x1c, 0x0d, 0xc0, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0x1a, 0x0d, 0x50, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0x22
 231         /*  DW_CFA_expression: r13 (r13) (DW_OP_lit8; DW_OP_minus; DW_OP_const4s: -64; DW_OP_and; DW_OP_const4s: -184; DW_OP_plus)  */
 232         .cfi_escape 0x10, 0x0d, 0x0e, 0x38, 0x1c, 0x0d, 0xc0, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0x1a, 0x0d, 0x48, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0x22
 233         /*  DW_CFA_expression: r14 (r14) (DW_OP_lit8; DW_OP_minus; DW_OP_const4s: -64; DW_OP_and; DW_OP_const4s: -192; DW_OP_plus)  */
 234         .cfi_escape 0x10, 0x0e, 0x0e, 0x38, 0x1c, 0x0d, 0xc0, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0x1a, 0x0d, 0x40, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0x22
 235                                 # LOE rbx r12 r13 r14 r15 zmm0
 236 
 237 /* Scalar math fucntion call
 238  * to process special input
 239  */
 240 
 241 L(SCALAR_MATH_CALL):
 242         movl      %r12d, %r14d
 243         movsd     64(%rsp,%r14,8), %xmm0
 244         call      tan@PLT
 245                                 # LOE rbx r14 r15 r12d r13d xmm0
 246 
 247         movsd     %xmm0, 128(%rsp,%r14,8)
 248 
 249 /* Process special inputs in loop */
 250         jmp       L(SPECIAL_VALUES_LOOP)
 251         cfi_restore(12)
 252         cfi_restore(13)
 253         cfi_restore(14)
 254                                 # LOE rbx r15 r12d r13d
 255 
 256 /* Auxilary branch
 257  * for out of main path inputs
 258  */
 259 
 260 L(AUX_BRANCH):
 261         vmovups   _dRangeVal+__svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %zmm14
 262 
 263 /*
 264  * Get the (2^a / 2pi) mod 1 values from the table.
 265  * Because doesn't have L-type gather, we need a trivial cast
 266  */
 267         lea       __svml_dtan_reduction_data_internal(%rip), %rax
 268         vmovups   %zmm1, (%rsp)
 269         vpternlogd $0xff, %zmm1, %zmm1, %zmm9
 270         vandpd    %zmm0, %zmm14, %zmm6
 271         vmovups   %zmm8, 64(%rsp)
 272         vcmppd    $4, {sae}, %zmm14, %zmm6, %k2
 273         vmovaps   %zmm9, %zmm5
 274         vpandq    .FLT_16(%rip){1to8}, %zmm11, %zmm8
 275         vpsrlq    $52, %zmm8, %zmm10
 276         vpsllq    $1, %zmm10, %zmm7
 277         vpaddq    %zmm10, %zmm7, %zmm4
 278         vpsllq    $3, %zmm4, %zmm0
 279         vpmovqd   %zmm0, %ymm3
 280         vpandnq   %zmm6, %zmm6, %zmm5{%k2}
 281         vcmppd    $3, {sae}, %zmm5, %zmm5, %k0
 282 
 283 /*
 284  * Break the P_xxx and m into 32-bit chunks ready for
 285  * the long multiplication via 32x32->64 multiplications
 286  */
 287         vpbroadcastq .FLT_19(%rip), %zmm6
 288         kxnorw    %k0, %k0, %k3
 289         kxnorw    %k0, %k0, %k4
 290         kxnorw    %k0, %k0, %k5
 291         kmovw     %k0, %edx
 292         vpxord    %zmm2, %zmm2, %zmm2
 293         vpxord    %zmm1, %zmm1, %zmm1
 294         vpxord    %zmm8, %zmm8, %zmm8
 295         vgatherdpd (%rax,%ymm3), %zmm2{%k3}
 296         vgatherdpd 8(%rax,%ymm3), %zmm1{%k4}
 297         vgatherdpd 16(%rax,%ymm3), %zmm8{%k5}
 298         vpsrlq    $32, %zmm2, %zmm5
 299         vpsrlq    $32, %zmm1, %zmm0
 300         vpsrlq    $32, %zmm8, %zmm13
 301 
 302 /*
 303  * Also get the significand as an integer
 304  * NB: adding in the integer bit is wrong for denorms!
 305  * To make this work for denorms we should do something slightly different
 306  */
 307         vpandq    .FLT_17(%rip){1to8}, %zmm11, %zmm15
 308         vpaddq    .FLT_18(%rip){1to8}, %zmm15, %zmm14
 309         vpsrlq    $32, %zmm14, %zmm7
 310         vpmullq   %zmm0, %zmm7, %zmm3
 311         vpandq    %zmm6, %zmm2, %zmm10
 312         vpandq    %zmm6, %zmm1, %zmm12
 313         vpandq    %zmm6, %zmm8, %zmm15
 314         vpandq    %zmm6, %zmm14, %zmm14
 315 
 316 /* Now do the big multiplication and carry propagation */
 317         vpmullq   %zmm10, %zmm7, %zmm4
 318         vpmullq   %zmm12, %zmm7, %zmm2
 319         vpmullq   %zmm13, %zmm7, %zmm1
 320         vpmullq   %zmm15, %zmm7, %zmm8
 321         vpmullq   %zmm5, %zmm14, %zmm7
 322         vpmullq   %zmm10, %zmm14, %zmm5
 323         vpmullq   %zmm0, %zmm14, %zmm10
 324         vpmullq   %zmm12, %zmm14, %zmm0
 325         vpmullq   %zmm13, %zmm14, %zmm12
 326         vpsrlq    $32, %zmm10, %zmm15
 327         vpsrlq    $32, %zmm0, %zmm13
 328         vpsrlq    $32, %zmm12, %zmm14
 329         vpsrlq    $32, %zmm5, %zmm12
 330         vpsrlq    $32, %zmm8, %zmm8
 331         vpaddq    %zmm14, %zmm1, %zmm1
 332         vpaddq    %zmm13, %zmm2, %zmm2
 333         vpaddq    %zmm15, %zmm3, %zmm15
 334         vpaddq    %zmm12, %zmm4, %zmm3
 335         vpandq    %zmm6, %zmm0, %zmm13
 336         vpaddq    %zmm1, %zmm13, %zmm4
 337         vpaddq    %zmm4, %zmm8, %zmm14
 338         vpsrlq    $32, %zmm14, %zmm0
 339         vpandq    %zmm6, %zmm10, %zmm10
 340         vpaddq    %zmm2, %zmm10, %zmm1
 341         vpaddq    %zmm1, %zmm0, %zmm8
 342 
 343 /*
 344  * Now round at the 2^-9 bit position for reduction mod pi/2^8
 345  * instead of the original 2pi (but still with the same 2pi scaling).
 346  * Use a shifter of 2^43 + 2^42.
 347  * The N we get is our final version; it has an offset of
 348  * 2^9 because of the implicit integer bit, and anyway for negative
 349  * starting value it's a 2s complement thing. But we need to mask
 350  * off the exponent part anyway so it's fine.
 351  */
 352         vpbroadcastq .FLT_22(%rip), %zmm1
 353         vpandq    %zmm6, %zmm7, %zmm7
 354         vpaddq    %zmm3, %zmm7, %zmm13
 355         vpsrlq    $32, %zmm8, %zmm3
 356         vpandq    %zmm6, %zmm5, %zmm5
 357         vpaddq    %zmm15, %zmm5, %zmm2
 358         vpaddq    %zmm2, %zmm3, %zmm15
 359         vpsrlq    $32, %zmm15, %zmm12
 360         vpaddq    %zmm13, %zmm12, %zmm5
 361 
 362 /* Assemble reduced argument from the pieces */
 363         vpandq    %zmm6, %zmm14, %zmm10
 364         vpandq    %zmm6, %zmm15, %zmm7
 365         vpsllq    $32, %zmm5, %zmm6
 366         vpsllq    $32, %zmm8, %zmm5
 367         vpaddq    %zmm7, %zmm6, %zmm4
 368         vpaddq    %zmm10, %zmm5, %zmm10
 369         vpsrlq    $12, %zmm4, %zmm6
 370 
 371 /*
 372  * We want to incorporate the original sign now too.
 373  * Do it here for convenience in getting the right N value,
 374  * though we could wait right to the end if we were prepared
 375  * to modify the sign of N later too.
 376  * So get the appropriate sign mask now (or sooner).
 377  */
 378         vpandq    .FLT_20(%rip){1to8}, %zmm11, %zmm0
 379         vpandq    .FLT_25(%rip){1to8}, %zmm10, %zmm13
 380         vpsllq    $28, %zmm13, %zmm14
 381 
 382 /*
 383  * Create floating-point high part, implicitly adding integer bit 1
 384  * Incorporate overall sign at this stage too.
 385  */
 386         vpxorq    .FLT_21(%rip){1to8}, %zmm0, %zmm8
 387         vporq     %zmm8, %zmm6, %zmm2
 388         vaddpd    {rn-sae}, %zmm2, %zmm1, %zmm12
 389         vsubpd    {rn-sae}, %zmm1, %zmm12, %zmm3
 390         vsubpd    {rn-sae}, %zmm3, %zmm2, %zmm7
 391 
 392 /*
 393  * Create floating-point low and medium parts, respectively
 394  * lo_23, ... lo_0, 0, ..., 0
 395  * hi_11, ... hi_0, lo_63, ..., lo_24
 396  * then subtract off the implicitly added integer bits,
 397  * 2^-104 and 2^-52, respectively.
 398  * Put the original sign into all of them at this stage.
 399  */
 400         vpxorq    .FLT_24(%rip){1to8}, %zmm0, %zmm6
 401         vporq     %zmm6, %zmm14, %zmm15
 402         vpandq    .FLT_27(%rip){1to8}, %zmm4, %zmm4
 403         vsubpd    {rn-sae}, %zmm6, %zmm15, %zmm8
 404 
 405 /*
 406  * If the magnitude of the input is <= 2^-20, then
 407  * just pass through the input, since no reduction will be needed and
 408  * the main path will only work accurately if the reduced argument is
 409  * about >= 2^-70 (which it is for all large pi multiples)
 410  */
 411         vpbroadcastq .FLT_31(%rip), %zmm14
 412         vandpd    .FLT_30(%rip){1to8}, %zmm11, %zmm15
 413         vpsrlq    $24, %zmm10, %zmm6
 414         vcmppd    $26, {sae}, %zmm14, %zmm15, %k6
 415         vcmppd    $22, {sae}, %zmm14, %zmm15, %k7
 416         vpxorq    .FLT_26(%rip){1to8}, %zmm0, %zmm1
 417         vpsllq    $40, %zmm4, %zmm0
 418         vporq     %zmm6, %zmm0, %zmm0
 419         vporq     %zmm1, %zmm0, %zmm4
 420         vsubpd    {rn-sae}, %zmm1, %zmm4, %zmm2
 421 
 422 /* Now add them up into 2 reasonably aligned pieces */
 423         vaddpd    {rn-sae}, %zmm2, %zmm7, %zmm13
 424         vsubpd    {rn-sae}, %zmm13, %zmm7, %zmm7
 425         vaddpd    {rn-sae}, %zmm7, %zmm2, %zmm3
 426         vaddpd    {rn-sae}, %zmm8, %zmm3, %zmm0
 427         vpbroadcastq .FLT_29(%rip), %zmm8
 428 
 429 /* Grab our final N value as an integer, appropriately masked mod 2^9 */
 430         vpandq    .FLT_23(%rip){1to8}, %zmm12, %zmm5
 431 
 432 /*
 433  * Now multiply those numbers all by 2 pi, reasonably accurately.
 434  * (RHi + RLo) * (pi_lead + pi_trail) ~=
 435  * RHi * pi_lead + (RHi * pi_trail + RLo * pi_lead)
 436  */
 437         vpbroadcastq .FLT_28(%rip), %zmm12
 438 
 439 /* The output is _VRES_Z (high) + _VRES_E (low), and the integer part is _VRES_IND */
 440         vpmovqd   %zmm5, %ymm4
 441         vmulpd    {rn-sae}, %zmm12, %zmm13, %zmm6
 442         vmovaps   %zmm12, %zmm10
 443         vfmsub213pd {rn-sae}, %zmm6, %zmm13, %zmm10
 444         vfmadd213pd {rn-sae}, %zmm10, %zmm8, %zmm13
 445         vpbroadcastq .FLT_34(%rip), %zmm10
 446         vfmadd213pd {rn-sae}, %zmm13, %zmm12, %zmm0
 447         vpbroadcastq .FLT_33(%rip), %zmm12
 448         vmovaps   %zmm9, %zmm8
 449         vpandnq   %zmm15, %zmm15, %zmm8{%k6}
 450         vpandnq   %zmm15, %zmm15, %zmm9{%k7}
 451         vandpd    %zmm11, %zmm9, %zmm9
 452         vandpd    %zmm6, %zmm8, %zmm14
 453         vorpd     %zmm14, %zmm9, %zmm6
 454         vandpd    %zmm0, %zmm8, %zmm9
 455         vmovdqu   .FLT_32(%rip), %ymm0
 456         vpsrlq    $32, %zmm6, %zmm5
 457         vpmovqd   %zmm5, %ymm5
 458         vpsrld    $31, %ymm5, %ymm1
 459         vpsubd    %ymm1, %ymm0, %ymm2
 460 
 461 /*
 462  *
 463  * End of large arguments path
 464  *
 465  * Merge results from main and large paths:
 466  */
 467         vmovups   (%rsp), %zmm1
 468         vpaddd    %ymm2, %ymm4, %ymm3
 469         vpsrld    $4, %ymm3, %ymm14
 470         vpslld    $4, %ymm14, %ymm7
 471         vpmovzxdq %ymm14, %zmm1{%k1}
 472         vpsubd    %ymm7, %ymm4, %ymm8
 473         vcvtdq2pd %ymm8, %zmm15
 474         vmovups   64(%rsp), %zmm8
 475         vfmadd231pd {rn-sae}, %zmm15, %zmm10, %zmm9
 476         vaddpd    {rn-sae}, %zmm6, %zmm9, %zmm13
 477         vfmadd213pd {rn-sae}, %zmm13, %zmm12, %zmm15
 478         vblendmpd %zmm15, %zmm8, %zmm8{%k1}
 479 
 480 /* Return to main vector processing path */
 481         jmp       L(AUX_BRANCH_RETURN)
 482                                 # LOE rbx r12 r13 r14 r15 edx zmm1 zmm8 zmm11
 483 END(_ZGVeN8v_tan_skx)
 484

 486         .align 64
